<tbody><tr>
<td style="width:50%; text-align:left;"><b><a href="/wiki/Speaker_of_the_United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="Speaker of the United States House of Representatives">Speaker</a> before election</b><br />
<p><a href="/wiki/Tip_O%27Neill" title="Tip O&#39;Neill">Tip O'Neill</a><br />
<a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democratic</a>
</p>
</td>
<td style="width:50%; text-align:right;"><b>Elected <a href="/wiki/Speaker_of_the_United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="Speaker of the United States House of Representatives">Speaker</a></b> <br />
<p><a href="/wiki/Jim_Wright" title="Jim Wright">Jim Wright</a><br />
<a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democratic</a>
</p>
</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The <b>1986 United States House of Representatives elections</b> was held on November 4, 1986, in the middle of <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Reagan" title="Ronald Reagan">Ronald Reagan</a>'s second term in office while he was still relatively popular with the American public. As in most midterm elections, the President's party—in this case, the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Republican_Party" class="mw-redirect" title="United States Republican Party">Republican Party</a> — lost seats, with the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Democratic_Party" class="mw-redirect" title="United States Democratic Party">Democratic Party</a> gaining a net of five seats and cementing its majority. These results were not as dramatic as those in the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate_elections,_1986" class="mw-redirect" title="United States Senate elections, 1986">Senate</a>, where the Republicans lost control of the chamber to the Democrats.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Retiring_incumbents">Retiring incumbents</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1986_United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Retiring incumbents">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Forty incumbents retired.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Democrats">Democrats</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1986_United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Democrats">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Nineteen incumbent Democrats retired.

<ol><li><span data-sort-value="Alabama07&#160;!"><a href="/wiki/Alabama%27s_7th_congressional_district" title="Alabama&#39;s 7th congressional district">Alabama&#160;7</a></span>: <a href="/wiki/Richard_Shelby" title="Richard Shelby">Richard Shelby</a>: To <a href="/wiki/1986_United_States_Senate_election_in_Alabama" title="1986 United States Senate election in Alabama">run for U.S. senator</a></li>
